The architecture follows a modular, extensible design with the following key components:\\n\\n## Abstract Interface\\nThe abstract CertValidator interface is defined in source/common/tls/cert_validator/cert_validator.h. It provides the base class with pure virtual methods: doVerifyCertChain (for asynchronous or synchronous certificate chain verification), addClientValidationContext (for client-side validation setup), and initializeSslContexts (for SSL context initialization).\\n\\n## Default Certificate Validator Implementation\\nThe DefaultCertValidator class in source/common/tls/cert_validator/default_validator.h implements the CertValidator interface with comprehensive X.509 chain verification support.
